# <a name="microsoft-365-encryption-chains"></a><span data-ttu-id="51a03-103">Cadeias de criptografia do Microsoft 365</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="51a03-103">Microsoft 365 encryption chains</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="51a03-104">O Microsoft 365 aproveita vários provedores de certificados diferentes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="51a03-104">Microsoft 365 leverages a number of different certificate providers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="51a03-105">A seguir descreve a lista completa de certificados raiz conhecidos do Microsoft 365 que os clientes podem encontrar ao acessar o Microsoft 365.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="51a03-105">The following describes the complete list of known Microsoft 365 root certificates that customers may encounter when accessing Microsoft 365.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="51a03-106">Para obter informações sobre os certificados que você pode precisar instalar em sua própria infraestrutura, consulte [Plan for third-party SSL certificates for Microsoft 365](../enterprise/plan-for-third-party-ssl-certificates.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="51a03-106">For information on the certificates you may need to install in your own infrastructure, see [Plan for third-party SSL certificates for Microsoft 365](../enterprise/plan-for-third-party-ssl-certificates.md).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="51a03-107">As informações de certificado a seguir se aplicam a todas as instâncias de nuvem nacionais e mundiais do Microsoft 365.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="51a03-107">The following certificate information applies to all worldwide and national cloud instances of Microsoft 365.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="51a03-108">Última atualização: **16/10/2020**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="51a03-108">Last updated: **10/16/2020**</span></span>
